-8 - pra . 3 . Avarwanapattikalonunna grUpu mUlakamula sWAnamunu vivariMcumu .
Avarwana pattikalo uwkqRtavAyu mUlakamula sWAnamu : hIliyaM , niyAn , ArgAn , kriptAn , jinAn , redAn anu Aru mUlakamulanu sunna grUpu mUlakamulu ani aMxuru .

redAni wappa migilinavi anniyu gAliyaMxu laBiMcunu .
meVMdalIP weVlipina Avarwana pattikalo I mUlakamulaku sWAnamulexu .
xInika kAraNamu meVMdalIP Avarwana pattikanu weVlipina samayamunaku 9 - I mUlakamulu kanugoVnabadalexu .
vItiniguriMci meVMdalIP kanIsamu prasWAvanaku kUdAwelexu .
kAvuna meVMdalIP Avarwana pattikalo I mUlakamulaku sWAnamunu kalpiMcalexu .
meVMdalIP AraMBa Avarwana pattikalo ( sunna grUpu mUlakamulu kanugoVnakamuMxu ) aXika qNavixyuxAwmakawa Xarmamulu gala grUpu VII mUlakamulaku ( helojanulaku ) veVnuveVMtane aXikaXana vixyuxAwmaka Xarmamulugala grUpu I mUlakamulu ( kRAra mUlakamulu ) uMdutanu oVka wIvramu ayina parivarwananu sUciMcucunnaxa .
I reVMdu grUpula maXyakoVnni ajFAwa mUlakamulu uMdavalayunanna sawyamunu appatilo SAswrajDulu XqDamugA viSvasiMcinAru .
WAm _san anu SAswrajDudu I mUlakamulanu guriMci UhAgAnamu jesinAdu .
waruvAwa grUpu mUlakamulu anniyu kanugoVnabadinavi .
mUlakamula Xarmamulanu anusariMci gurwiMcina nAlugu weVgalalonu moVxati vAnilo I uwkqRtavAyu mUlakamulu unnavi .
eVlaktrAn vinyAsamunu AXAramu jesukoVni mUlakamulanu nAlugu vargamulugA viBajiMcadamEnaxi .
I vargIkaraNamu prakAramu I mUlakamulanu ( hIliyaM minahA ) P blAku mUlakamulugA parigaNiMcadamEnaxi .
xIniki kAraNamu I mUlakamu lanniMtiyaMxunu veruparace eVlaktrAn P arcitAl _loniki praveSiMcunu .
hIliyaM minahA migilina mUlakamula paramANuvu lanniMtiyaMxunu velansI kakRyalalo 8 eVlaktrAnulu BarwI ayi unnavi .
hIliyaM mAwramu reVMdu eVlaktrAn _lawo BarwI ayi unnaxi .
viswrawa nEtrojan prawi pIriyad civara uwkqRNavAyu mUlakamu uMdunu .
ixi cAla arWavaMwamu ayina viRayamu .
prawi pIriyad _lonu moVtaxavaccu kRAramUlakamu yoVkka eVlaktrAn vinyAsamu nsi ayi unnaxi .
paramANu saMKya peVrigina koVlaxi eVlaktrAn _lu s ArbitAl _ la lonu , waruvAwa p ArbitAl _lonu praveSiMci civaraku pIriyad ns2 np6 vinyAsamuwo mugiyucunnaxi .
kAvuna uwkqRNa vAyu mUlakamulu anniMtini pIriyad _lalo civara uMcadaM cAla samarWanIyamugA unnaxi .

18 - saMkRipwa samAXAna praSnalu pra. 1 . uwkqRta vAyumUlakamula eVlaktrAn vinyAsamunu weVlupumu .

22 - 2 . loha saMgrahaNamu pra . 1 . Kanijamu anagA nemi ? Kanijamulanu SuxXiceyutaku upayogiMcu sAmAnya BOwika vixAnamulanu vivariMpumu .

SuxXiceyuta : - BUminuMdi wIyabadina mudiKanijamu matti , isuka , gulakarAyi moVxalagu malinamulawo kalasi uMdunu .

pra . 2 . loha saMgrahaNamulo upayogiMcu viviXa rakamulagu koVlumulanu varNiMcumu .

leVd mAwramu AksIkaraNamu ceVMxi leVd monAksEd _gA mArunu .

8 ) vixyuxviSleRaNamu : I viXAnamuvalana pariSuxXamagu lohamunu poVMxavaccunu .

9 ) maMdala SoXanamu : I paxXawini upayogiMci lohamulaku awyaMwaSuxXawanu cekUrcavaccunu .

kaddI rUpamugA unna lohamunu poVdavugA unna oVka silikA vadavalo patamulo cUpina viXamugA amarcavalayunu .

vixyuw pravahiMcutavalana uRNamu veVluvadunu .
uRNamuvalana A BAgamunaMxali lohamu Skarugunu .
I sWiwilo preraNa veRtamunu kramamugA reVMdava civaraku jarupavalayunu .

I viXAnamunu anekasArlu wirigi wirigi cesina civaraka awiSuxXamagu lohamu laBiMcunu .
-34 - pra . 4 . AksEd , kArbanet , salPEd KanijamulanuMdi lohamulanu wayAruceyu sAmAnya rasAyanika viXAnamulanu vivariMpumu .
1 . AksEd _ Kanijamunu lohamunuMdi veruceyuta : a ) kRayakaraNa paxXawi : AksEd Kanijamunu kok , kArban monAksEd moVxalagu kRayakariNilawo vedicesinappudu ani kRayakaraNamunoVMxi lohamulugA mArunu .

pawrika woVlixaSalo pE ixxaru saMpAxakulaku koVdAli SivarAma kqRNayya cexodu vAxodugA uMdevAru , AnAdu xeSaMlo neVlakoVnna rAjakIya , sAMGika parisWiwulanubatti kqRNA pawrika kUdA miwavAxa XoraNilone nadicexi .

prawI rojU sAyaMwraM pUta , sarasamAde velYa , A sAhiwI xarbAru prAraMBamyayexata - sWAnaMlokqRNArAvugAru - vacci ASInulayyevArata - " guru graMWaM sAheVb " ani peru peVttukoVni , xarbArulo pannIti jallulu kuripiswU , xarbAru SAyar , kAtUri veVMkateSvar _ ceVppina I paxyaM cirasmaraNIyaM .
" perolagammu xarbArulo nIvuMda DillIlo xarbAru dillavoyeV maswakammuna Svewa makuta mIvu XariMpa naswamiMcLri kirItAXipawulu gAMBIrya guNamunin gana gUdutaM jesi jalaXilo rAcabAtalu rahiMceV mOna muxriwa Bava raxAnana muxra BU prajalaku vAcAla wApraBa moVsaMgeV - o guru graMXa sAheVba! uxaXivalayi wAvanI cakramoVlla nI yaxviwIya maMxahAsa SAsanamunu mOlYixAlci melaramAduwa pannIti yolalAta - " A xarbArulone , veNugopAl , natarAj , viGneSvara , vagErA - yiwara SiXila SilA vigrahAluMdevi .
I mutnUrivAri xarbArulo , viviXa SAswrAlalo uxxaMdulu , sakala kalYABijFulu , navarasAlanaMxiMce kavi , - - gAyaka , paMdiwa , nata , hAsya , cakravarwulaMxarU ; bahu viRaya sekaraNaXArulE - potIllo pAraMgawulE - grAma sWAyi nuMdi - varaku wAjA vArwalanu gaxya , paxya , nAtaka prakriyalalo eVppatikappudu prawiniwyaM vacci ; ceVppevArata .
vAraMxiMcina vArwalannitina pariSIliMci AlociMci - vyAKyala rUpaMlo - rUpaMlo - saMxarBociwaMgA rAsi caxuvarulakaMxiMcevAru kqRNArAvugAru .
xarbArulo kqRNarAyuni samAna PAyagA , BogarAju vAroVkkare kUrcuni , samAyanukUlaMgA vakwagA vyavahariMceVdivArata .
akkadaku adavi bApirAju , kola veVnnu rAmakoteSvararAvu , piMgalYi nAgeMxrarAvu , mallAxi rAmakqRNaSAswri , xAmarAju , BAvarAju narasiMhArAvu , goparAju , puvvAda SeRagirirAvu , gurujAda rAGava Sarma , munimANikyaM narasiMhArAvu , beVjavAda gopAlareVddi , rAvUri vAru marikeVMxaro prawi niwyaM hAjarayyevArata - govAda nirIkRaNarAvu ( BAgyanagar eVditar ) kUdA hAjarayyovAdata .
aMwaku pUrvaM Ayana peru sAmelugA vuMdexata - Ayana xarbAruku rAvadaM AlasyaM ayinaMxuvalla kqRmArAvugAru hAsyaMgA " emayyA - - nI kosaraM nirIkRiswu vunnAM .
iMwa sepu eVkkadaku veVlYlYAv " ani ; praSniMcAdata - nuMdi xarbArulo Ayana rAgAne , nirIkNaNarAvu , nirIkNiMcakuMdAne vaccAdani ane vArata - valla wanu A nirIkRaNarAvu perune sArWakaM cesukunnAnani Ayane svayaMgA macilI patnaMlo oVka niMdu saBalo ceVppadaM jarigiMxi .
akkada ( xarbArulo ) kaviwvaM , gAnaM , vexAMwaM , nqwyaM , ciwraleKanaM , saMgIwaM - - , lokaMloni vArwalu annI viRayAlapEna carcalu kakoVnasAgevata - pattABigAru mAwraM unnappudu kevalaM rAjakIyAlake praWama sWAnaM uMdexi .
bApirAjugAru pAtalu , jAnapaxageyAlu pAduwU , adugulu vesevArata .
ciwraleKanaM , SilpaM moVxalEna viRayAlu praswAviswunnappudu bApirAjugAru eVMwo uxrekaMwo mAtlAdevAru .
maro roju kAtUri vAri , pannIti jallulu , jadivAnalu kuripiMcevArata - muni mANikyaM vAri hAsyokwulu weneVlUre , weVlugu BARalo vyaMgyAnni raMgariMci aMxarikI , A mAXuryAnni paMcevAdata - nAdu piMgalYivAri nAtaka kalYopanyAsAlu , oVka saMxeSa samayaMlo mallAxivAri sAhiwya rahasyAlu , maXya , maXya - - jaruk SAswrigAri peradIlu viMtU - uwsAhaparuswU - , avasaramanukunnappudu camawkariswU wama aXyakRa sWAna gOravAnni nilabeVttukuMtU uMde vArata mUtnUri vAru .
Ayana xarbAruku rAvadame wama axqRtaMgA BAviMcevArata A rojullo .
koVMxaru saMxeSAlu wIsukoVni veVlYlYevArata - saMxeSAla naMxiMci veVlYlYevArata - OwsAhika kavulaMxarU wAmu exi rAsinA , weVcci xarbArulo caxavAlani carcalo pAlgoVni wama sawwA welcukovAlani ubalAta padevArata .
ayiwe - - vArEnA aMxarikI praveSaM - axqRta BAgyaM labiMcexata - asmaxIyulu - wasmaxIyulane Bexa BAvaM akkada maccukEnA kanabadexi kAxata .
A vixaMgAne - kaviwAMSaloni maMci - saxvivimarSalugA koVnasAgevita - gammawwo kAnI ; mana
kqRNArAvu gAru wala Upiwe cAlu , wama axqRtaM paMdinatle bAviMcevArata vAru .
beVjavAda gopAlareVddi gAru ravIMxruni racanala nuMdi anuvaxiMcina ` ciwrAMgaxa ' graMWAnni xarbArulo caxivi - vinipiMci , " SeVBAR " anipiMcukuni , kqRNarAyuni kalaM nuMdi rAse axqRtAniki nocukunnAru .
- - A xarbAruloki saByulu rAvadaM eVMwo wamARAgA uMdexi .
kilakila navvulawo , kitakita lAduwU oVkosAri saByulaMxarU , oVkkasAre lopaliki vaccevArata .
oVkappudu bucci suMxararAma SAswrigAru vaccevAru .
vArini jUdagAne , navvulu vinipiMcevi .
Ayana mAwraM peVxavi , vippevAru kAxu .
poVduM mukku wuducukovadame gAni iMwalone ; " vaMkAya woVdimalo vaMkarela " aMtU jaruk SAswri vaccevArata .
asalu A xarbArunu varNiMcadaM aMwa suluvEna panemI kAxu .
eVMxukaMte - xarbAru rojuko mAxirigA mAripowUMdexita - kavi puMgavulu , natulu , gAyakulu , ciwrakArulu , saMpAxakulu , pAwrikeyulu , saMGa sevA parAyaNulu , xIna janulu , sinIxarSakulu , rAjakIya pramuKulu , racayiwalu , , anaXikArlu ; paMdiwule kAxu , pAmarulu sEwaM xarbAruku vaccevArata - eVMxareVMxaro , .
hAjaravuwUMdevArata - e roju kAroju kroVwwa xanaMwo niMdugA - wqpwigA - AnaMxaMgA - AhlAxaMgA koVluvu nUwana aMSAlawo , goRTi kAryakramAlawo alariMcexi .
AxariMcexi - cUpiMcexata - sawkariMcexata - prowsahiMcexata - kqRNarAyani xarbAru veVnneVla jallulu kuripiMci , paluku muwyAla woraNAlu katti , pasidi vipaMci wIgalu - - mIti BARA sarasvawini arpiMci , veVlaleni kAnukalaMxiMci , wulaleni bogAlanu samarpiMci murusukoVMxi " ani oVkaru rASAru .
axi sawyamani ; I nAtiki BAvarAjugAru , dAktaru kuppA veVMkatrAma SAswrigAru , pidugu rAmaliMgayyagAru ( jarnalist ) moVxalagu peVxxalaMtU uMtAru .
xarbAruku pEna uxahariMcinavAru gAka ; gudiseva subbayya , kASInAWuni pUrNa malliKArdunudu , goVttipAti brahmayya , paMdiwa goVrreVpAti veMkata subbayya , rAvUri veVMkata sawyanArAyaNa , peVnumarwi , cigurupAti , ayyYyaMki vAralu xarbAru saxasyakotiloni vAre .
" BojarAja sanniXiki newa neyuxevAMgi veVlYlYinappudu , awaniki , " kavayAmi , vayAmi , yAmi " anu kaviwva xoraNi kaliginatlu ; mutnUri vAri sAnnixyaMlo unnavAriki , pawrikA vyAsaracanA xuraMXarawvaM labiMcutalo AScarya memuMxani " Ayana SiRyuloVkarannAru .
axi mummUrwulA nijamEna sawyaM .
A kovaloni vAre , kota subbArAvu , kamalAkara veVMkatrAvu , rAvUri veVMkata sawyanArAyaNa rAvu , viSvanAWa veVMkateSvarlu - nArla veVMkateSvararAvu , eVMxaro uMdevArata .
- - kqRNarAvu gAri maMciwanaM maMci gaMXaMlAMtixi .
maMciwanaMlo nuMde mamawa laBiswuMxi .
mamawalo nuMdi samawa , samawanuMdi ; sOBrAwqwvaM xAninuMdi niRkalmaRawvaM , xAninuMdi viSAla mAnava xqkpaXaM - erpadevi Ayana sAmIpyaMlo .
A mOna muxrAlaMkAruni jFAna maMxiraMlo mUga pUjAru leVMxaro uMdevArata ! - xarbAru biruxulu : britiRu praBuwva pAlanA kAlaMlo pramuKulEna praBuwvoxyogulaku , ASriwulaku ; AMgla saMvawsarAxina , lexA cakravarwi janmaxinamagu jUn oVkatava wexIna biruxuliswU uMdevAru .
I biruxulakosaM koVMxaru uvvilYlYUruwuMdevAru .
alA biruxa praxAnaM jarige rojulalo mutnUri kqRNArAvugAru ceVrukuvAda veVMkata narasiMhaM paMwulu gAru xarbAru hAlulo kUrcunnappudu mana pawrika warapuna kUda biruxulanu pawrikalo pracurixxAmannAru narasiMhaM gAru .
" BeR " annAru kqRNArAvugAru .
praWamaMgA taMgutUri prakASaM paMwulu gAriki " AMXra siMha " ane biruxunu sUciMcAru ceVruku vAdavAru .
veVMtana kqRNArAvu gAru ` ' SabxaM kaMte - - ` ' SabxaM samuciwaMgA uMtuMxani yocana cesi , " AMxra kesari " prakASaM annAru .
A SuBamuhUrwaM nuMce ` AMXra kesari ' biruxu xeSaM naluceVragulA pAkiMxi .

nyApawi nArAyaNa mUrwigAru : ` aKilAMXra kewakI - ' 11 . xuvvUri subbammagAru : - ` xeSa bAMXavi ' .

alAge oVkasAri , kqRNArAvu gAru oVka miwruni iMtiki , xevawArcana keVlYlYArata - marikoVMwa maMxi kUdA unnArata - kqRNArAvu gAri walamIxa aMxarikaMte mariMwa eVkkuvagA xivyoxakaM yiMtivAru callArata - waruvAwa yivawalaku vaccina kqRNArAvu gAru , wama miwrulawo " nA mIxa wIrWaM eVkkuvagA eVMxukaBiRekaM ceSAro weVlusA ? 1 . rAjanIwi SAswramu BAvAlu , sixXAMwAlu , saMsWalu aXyAyamu . 1 paricayamu 1 . rAjanIwi SAswrasvaBAvAnni , xAni aBivqxXini vivariMpumu .

atti nagara rAjyAla nirmANaM , nagara rAjyamulaloni praBuwva svarUpamu , aMxali rAjakIya saMsWalu , vAti viXulanu guriMci aXyayanaM ceyu SAswrAnni " rAjanIwiSAswraM " gA vAru pilavadaM jarigiMxi .

axi rAjanIwi BAvAla KajAnA " .
svaBAvamu : aristAtil aBiprAyaMlo " mAnavudu saMGajIvi " vyakwiki saMGamuwo vidaxIyarAni saMbaMXamunnaxi .
nixra , Akalixappulu vyakwiki eVlA sahaja prapawwulo saMGajIvanamukUda aMwe , oVMtariwanamunu vyakwi BariMcaledu .
aMxuke " e vyakwi saMGamulo jIviMcaledo leka svayaM samqxXi cewa eVvadiki saMGajIviwamu avasaramulexo awadu wappaka paSuvugAni leka BagavaMwudugAni ayiuMdAli " ani rAjanIwiSAswra piwAmahudEna aristAtil perkoVneVnu .
2 . samAjamuloni prawivyakwilo eVMwo koVMwa svArWamuMdunu .
wana korikalanu , lakRyAlanu neVravercukoVnutaku niraMwaramu kqRi salputa mAnavula sahaja lakRaNamu .
mAnavulalo svArWamu , krUrawvamu , kapatamu , asUya , asahanamu moVxalagu ceVdu guNAlukUda unnavi .
vIni PaliwamugA vyakwula maXya saMGarRaNa janiMcunu .
oVka vyakwi aBimawAlu , aBilARalu veroVkari aBimawAlu , aBilARalaku BinnamugA uMdadame kAkuMda saMGamulo viviXa vyakwula korikalu oVkaxAnikoVkati addaMkigA nuMduta valana itti saMGarRaNa janiMcunu .
itti saMGarRaNa woVlagiMci saMGajIviwAnni kramabaxXaMcesi purogawini sAXiMcutaku saMGamuloni vAraMxaru koVnni niyamAlu pAtiMcuta avasaramu .
itti niyamAlanu rUpoVMxiMcutaku , amalu ceyutaku saMGatiwamEna oVka aXikAramu avasaramu .
oVka praxeSamuloni prajalu itti niyamAlanu rUpoVMxicutaku , vAtini amalu ceyadAniki oVka vyakwiki gAni , koVMwamaMxi vyakwulaku gAni aXikAramu iccinapudu atti vyakwula samuxAyamu praBuwvamu anabadunu .
oVka nirNIwa praxeSamulo prajalu wAmu niyamiMcukoVnna praBuwvAniki , viXeyulE A praBuwvAniki , A BUBAgamuloni prajalanu , saMsWalanu SAsiMce sArvaBOmAXikAramu uMte xAnini rAjyamaMxuru .
itti rAjyamu , praBuwvamula guriMci vyakwiki vAtiwogala saMbaMXamunu guriMci vivariMcunaxe rAjanIwi SAswramu .
aristAtil uxxeSaMlo mAnavudu saMGajIvi mAwrame gAka " rAjakIyajIvi " kUda .
vyakwi jIvanaMlo rAjakIya jIvanaM kUdA aMwarBAgame . mAnavudu wana vyakwiwva vikAsAniki avasaramayina saMsWala neVnniMtino neVlakoVlpukoVnnAdu .
rAjyamukUda alAMti saMsWalalo oVkati .

5 . itIvali kAlaMlo rAjanIwiSAswraMlo sAMpraxAyika vEKarulaku BinnaMgA vyavasWApaka vEKari , pravarwanAvAxa vEKari , uwpAxaka , uwpAxiwa vEKari moVxalagu vEKarulu , SiRtula sixXAMwamu krIdA sixXAMwamu , pravarwanAvAxa sixXAMwamu moVxalagu aXyayana paxXawulu cerAyi .

2 . prAcIna grIkula rAjanIwi aBiprAyAlanu vivariMpumu .
. lexA . prAcIna grIkula praXAna rAjanIwi BAvanalanu klupwaMgA weVlupumu .

1 . grIkula aBiprAyaMlo vyakwi jIvanamu , sAMGika jIvanamu veruveru kAxu .

3 . pOrasawvamu : grIkulu " pOrasawvamu " ane paxAnni parimiwamEna arWaMlo vAdAru .

aMxuvalanane peVrikils . " prajI vyavahArAlalo curukugA pAlgoVnani vyYakwini memu panikirAnivAnigA parigaNiswAmu " ani perkoVnnAdu .

1 . viviXa rAjakIya paxAla arWa vivaraNa : vAdukaBARalo prawivyakwi aneka rAjanIwi paxAlaku arWamu weVliyakapoyinA vAtini vAduwAdu .

16 - sAmrAjya vAxamu valasa viXAnamuvaMti neti aMwarjAwIya samasyala avagAhanaku , agra rAjyAla pravarwananu arWaM cesukovatAniki rAjanIwiSAswra sixXAMwAla aXyayanaM wodpaduwuMxi .

5 . rAjanIwi SAswramu kalYA . SAswramA . carciMpudu .
. lexA . rAjanIwi SAswramu eVMwavaraku SAswramo carciMpudu .

1 . prakqwi leka BOwika SAswrAlu , 2 . sAMGika SAswrAlu , prakqwi leka BOwika SAswrAlaloni viRayAlanu anni saMxarBAlalonu nirUpaNa ceyavaccunu .

19 . aXyAyaM . 3 rAjanIwiSAswra aXyayana paxXawulu 6 . rAjanIwiSAswra aXyayana paxXawulanu vivariMpumu .

1 . cAriwraka paxXawi heVnrImeVyin : rAjanIwiSAswra aXyayanaMlo cAriwraka paxXawiki prAXAnyawa niccina vArilo heVnrI meVyin , lAskI , sIlI , prImas , mArks . muKyulu .

20 . kAni sidj .vik ceVppinatlu praswuwa samasyanu pariRkariMcukoVnutalo cAriwraka paxXawi upayogapadaxu .

2 . pariSIlanAwmaka paxXawi : pariSIlanAwmaka paxXawiki aXika prAXAnyawa niccivAdu lArd .brEs .

4 . prayogAwmaka paxXawi : kAtlin moV//vAru I paxXawiki prAXAnyawa niccAru .

kAni rAjanIwi SAswraMlo anusariMce prayogAwmaka paxXawi 22 . nanusariMci rUpoVMxiMcabade sixXAMwAlu nirxuRtamayinavigA BAviMca vIlulexu .

5 . SAswrIyapaxXawi : I paxXawinanusariMcuta xvArA SAswra sixXAMwAlanu spaRtaMgA arWaMcesukovaccunu .

6 . wAwvika paxXawi : pE aXyayana paxXawula xvArA pariSIlana jaripi , viSleRaNAwmakaMgA koVnni prAWamika sUwrAlanu rUpoVMxiMcukovaccunu .

ayiwe I Uha koVnni paryAyAlu wappu kAvaccukUda .

pleto wana ripablik graMWaMlo AxarSa rAjya rUpakalpana ceSAdu .
iMxulo vAswavikawaku wAvuMdaxu .
vAswavAlaku saMbaMXamuleni AxarSAla valla prayojanamemi uMdaxu .
kAvuna rAjanIwi SAswra aXyayanamu e oVkka paxXawilonu sAgaxu .

alAge rAjanIwi wawwvavewwa vAswavikawa nAXAraMgAne wana wAwwvika ciMwananu prAraMBiMcavaleV .

23 . 7 . rAjanIwi SAswraM patla AXunika vEKarulni vivariMcaMdi .
rAjanIwiSAswra aXyayanaMlo gala vEKarulu reVMdu rakAlu .
avi sAMpraxAyika , AXunika vEKarulu .
AXunika vEKarulu kriMxa perkoVnabadinavi .
avi : A . samAjaSAswra vEKari .
B . manaswawvaSAswra vEKari .
C . ArWika pariNAwmaka vEKari .
D . vyavasWApaka vEKari E . pravarwanAvAxa vEKari A . samAjaSAswra vEKari : devid Istan , meVkEvar , almaMd .lu I vEKariki prAXAnyawaniccAru .
rAjyamanexi rAjakIya saMsWagA kaMte sAmAjika saMsWagAne eVkkuvagA unnaxani veVbar vaMti rAjanIwi SAswrajFula aBiprAyamu .
mAnavula rAjakIya kAryakalApAla avagAhanaku sAmAjika avagAhana cAlA praXAnamEnaxi .
samAjaMlo mAwrame oVkavyakwi hoxAnu anuBaviMcadAniki , oVka pAwranu nirvahiMcadAniki vIlavuwuMxi .
samAjaSAswra vEKari " rAjakIya saMskqwi " anepaxAnni vyApwiloka weVcciMxi .
samAja saByulugA vyakwulu nercukoVnna viviXa aMSAle rAjakIya saMskqwigA parigaNiMcabadinaxi .
oVka rAjya rAjakIya kAryakalApAlanu samAjaMloni viviXa saMsWalu , bqMxAlu praBAviwaM ceswAyi .
kAvuna , prawyeka prayojana bqMxAlanu guriMcina aXyayanaM , pariSoXana ceyAlani samAjaSAswra vEKari sUciswuMxi .
B . manaswawvaSAswra vEKari : AXunika kAlaMlo rAjanIwiSAswraM manaswawva SAswrAniki bAgA sannihiwamayiMxi .
manaswawvaSAswra vEKariki prAXAnyawaniccina vArilo rAbart eV. cArleVs grAhaMvAleVs , lAsveVl moVxalagu vAru pramuKulu , hAbs . , mAkiyaveVllI vaMti AXunika yugAraMBaMloni SAswravewwalu vyakwi manaswawva lakRaNAlawone wama wawvaciMwananu prAraMBiMcAru .
24 . vyakwiloni guNAlu , alavAtlu , uxrekAlu , sahaja pravqwwulu moVxalagu aMSAla pAwranu pariSIliMcadAniki manaswawvaSAswra vEKari upayogapaduwuMxi .
nedu rAjanIwi SAswraMlo ` aXikAraM . guriMcina BAvana manaswawvaSAswra vEKari prAXAnyawanu peVMcivesiMxi .
rAjanIwi SAswraM aXikAraM . xAni arjanaku prAXAnyawa niswunnaxi .
dablyu.eV.rAbsan xaRtilo aXikArAnni haswagawaM cesukovadaM , xAnini nilupukovadaM rAjanIwiSAswra praXAna lakRyamu .
lAsveVl mariyu kAplAn .la aBiprAyaMlo " rAjyamuwo rUpoVMxu aXikAra rUpakalpananu guriMci , atti aXikAra viniyogamunu guriMci anuBava pUrvakaMgA vicAraNaceyu SAswrame rAjanIwi SAswramu .
lAsveVl , beVtrAMd rasseVl moVxalagu vAru rAjanIwi yoVkka kriyAsakwini gUrci ceVbuwU rAjanIwilo aXikArame praXAnAMSamaMtAru .
aXikAramu , xAnimUlamu , svaBAvamu , pariXi moVxalagu vAti aXyayaname rAjanIwiyani rAjyAXikAra Arjanaku , xAnini nilabeVttukovadAniki cese porAtame rAjanIwilo praXAnamani aMtAru .
I . aXikAra . BAvana sAMpraxAya vEKari BinnamEnaxi .
koVMxari aBiprAyaMlo manaswawva vEKariki samAnArWaM " aXikAra vEKari" .
C . ArWika pariNAwmaka vEKari : uwpawwi , paMpiNI viXAnAlanu rAjyaM kramabaxXaM ceswuMxi .
I vEKari xvArA uxAravAxaM soRalijala , kamyUnijaM vaMti aneka AlocanA viXAnAlu AvirBaviMcAyi .
rAjyaM ArWika kAryakalApAlanu nirvahiMcadaM wappanisari .
krameNA rAjya ArWika kAryakalApAlu peVruguwunnavi .
kAvuna ArWika pariNAwmaka vEKari rAjanIwiSAswraMlo cotu cesukunnYaxi .
kArl . mArks . , J.S.mil vaMti rAjanIwi SAswravewwalu rAjakIyArWaSAswraM guriMci viviXa graMWAlu raciMcAru .
kArl .mArks . aBiprAyaMlo ArWikaparamEna Sakwulu cariwranu nadipiswAyani , rAjakIya sAmAjika mArpulaku ave kAraNamani perkoVnnAdu .
anni rAjakIya , sAmAjika mArpulaku , viplavAlaku asalu kAraNAlanu uwpawwi , paMpiNI viXAnAlaloni mArpulalone anveRiMcAli .
rAjanIwi SAswramu patla ArWika paramEna vEKari anagA ixiye .
D . vyavasWApaka vEKari : oVka vyavasWa pUrwi avagAhanaku A vyavasWa viSleRaNa avasaraM .
vyavasWa ane BAvanalo A vyavasWaloni mUlakAlannI oVkaxAniwo oVkati laMkeV vesikoVni , parassarAXAriwaMgA unnAyane arWaM imidi unnaxi .
25 . vEKari prakqwi vijFAnaSAswrAla nuMdi grahiMcabadinaxi .
devid Istan , almaMd kAplAn .lu I vEKarini viviXa rAjakIya vyavasWala viSleRaNaku upayogiMcAru .
viviXa viRaya BAgAlaku ceVMxina vyavasWalanu oVka sAmAnya BAvana xvArA arWaM cesukoVni , A avagAhana AXAraMgA oVka sAXAraNa sixXAMwAnni rUpoVMxiMcadaM I vEKari lakRyamu .
I vEKari rAjakIya vyavasWanu kriyASIla xqkpaXaMwo vIkRiswuMxi .
I vEKarilo ` vyavasWa . lapE pUrwi keMxrIkaraNa uMtuMxi .
devid Istan vaMtivAru ` rAjakIya vyavasWa . ane BAvananu praveSapeVttAru .
E . pravarwanAvAxa vEKari : rAjanIwiSAswra aXyayana paxXawulalo pravarwanAvAxa paxXawi oVkati .
I vEKari AXunikamEnaxi .
reVMdava prapaMca yuxXAnaMwaramu ameVrikA rAjanIwiSAswrajFulu pracAramuloki wIsukoVnivaccina kroVwwapaMWA pravarwanAvAxa vEKari .
moVxati prapaMca yuxXAnaMwaramu PrAMk keVMt anu ameVrikA pawrikA racayiwa rAjakIya pravarwana anu SIrRikawo oVka graMWAnni pracuriMcAdu .

211 - kAlRiyam prameyAlu : eVmukalu , xaMwAlu peVragadAniki , erpadina eVmukalu gatti padatAniki kAlRiyaM kAvalasi uMxi .

garBasWa SiSuvu eVmukala nirmANAniki , rakwa samqxXiki garBiNI swrIki kAlRiyam avasaraM eVMwo uMxi .
prasava samayaMlo kAlRiyam avasaraM eVkkuva .
biddaku pAlicce walli SarIraMlo pAlu wayAru kAvadAniki kAlRiyam avasaraM .
aMwe kAkuMdA prasava samayaMlo kolpoyina kAlRiyam _ SarIra wirigi kUda beVttukovAli .
iMxu valla pAlicce walliki kAlRiyam avasaraM cAlA 212 - eVkkuva .
viviXa xaSalalo unna vAriki rojuku kAvalasina kAlRiyam mowAxulu anubaMXa pattikalo cUdavaccu .
kAlRiyam _ nyUnawArogAlu : eVmukala nirmANaM , peVruguxalaku kAlRiyaM avasaraM ganuka AhAraMlo ixi lopiMcinappudu SarIraM peVruguxala kuMtupaduwuMxani pariSoXanalu rujuvu cesAyi .
pillalalo kAlRiyam lopiswe rikeVts ane vyAXi saMBaviswuMxi .

rakwaM wvaragA gadda kattaxu .

213 - PAsparas : SarIraMlo PAsParas oVka muKyamEna Kanija paxArWaM SarIraMloni moVwwaM Kanija lavaNAla lo ixi 22 SAwaM uMtuMxi .

ivi kUdA nirjIva vaswuvule kAbatti , ivi kUdA wama viluvakannA eVkkuva viluvani sarukuki ivvavu .
` Srama ' jaragadaM annA , ` vuwpawwi ' jaragadaM annA oVkate kAbatti , " Srama sAXanAlu " annA , " vuwpawwi sAXanAlu " annA , oVkate , ` Srama sAXanAlu ' annA , ` Srama parikarAlu ' annA , ` vuwpawwi sAXanAlu ' annA ` vuwpawwi parikarAlu ' annA - I 4 mAtalakU oVkate arWaM .
Sramacese maniRi wana cewiloki e parikarAlu wIsukuni pani ceswAdo vAtini mAwrame ( suwwI , kawweVrA , maggaM , nAgalI , raMpaM 38 - lAMti vAtini mAwrame ) " Srama parikarAlu " anadaM BARalo oVka alavAtu .
nijAniki ` sAXanaM ' annA , ` parikaraM ' annA oVkate .
Srama jaragadAniki kAvalasina prawIxI Srama sAXaname .
Srama parikarame .
mudi paxArWAlu lekapoyinA Srama jaragaxu , Srama parikarAlu lekapoyinA Srama jaragaxu , AgjilarI paxArWAlu lekapoyinA Srama jaragaxu .
kAbatti ivannI kUdA Srama jaragadAniki kAvalasina sAXanAle .
aMxuke , I vaswuvulannitinI kalipi oVke mAtawo " Srama sAXanAlu " ano " vuwpawwi sAXanAlu " ano anavaccu .
oVka vaswuvu , mudipaxArWaM ayinA , AgjilarI paxArWaM ayinA , Srama parikaraM ayinA xAnni oVka panilo vAdinappudu , axi wana viluvakannA oVkka aNuvaMwa kUdA eVkkuva viluvani koVwwa sarukuki cercaxu .
I viRayaMlo Srama sAXanAlannI oVke svaBAvaMwo vuMtAyi .
batta peVttubadixArudiki battaxvArA vaccina 20 lABAniki e aMSaM kAraNamA ani cUswunnAM kaxA ? mudipaxArWaM kAraNaM kAxani iMwaku muMxu weliMxi .
ippudu , Srama sAXanAlu kUdA kAraNaM kAxani weliMxi .
peVttubadixArudu , mudipaxArWaM mIxa 30 peVdiwe , xAnixvArA battaki 30 viluva mAwrame vaswuMxi .
alAge , iwara Srama sAXanAlanniti mIxA 50 peVdiwe vAtixvArA battaki 50 mAwrame vaswuMxi .
aMte ippatiki battaki ceriMxi 30 = 80 viluva .
kAnI , battalo moVwwaM 120 viluva vuMxi .
aMte , mudipaxArWAnikI , iwara Srama sAXanAlakI saMbaMXaM lekuMdA cerina viluva iMkA 40 vuMxi .
ika manaku migilina aMSaM A battani wayAru ceVyyadaMlo pani cesina SrAmikulu .
I SrAmikulakU , battalovunna I 40 viluvakI eVlA saMbaMXamo ippudu cUxxAM .
39 - SrAmikulu wama ` jIwAla ' viluvakannA eVkkuva viluva ivvagalarA ?
peVttubadixArudu mudipaxArWaM mIxa eVMwa KarcupeVdiwe , xAni xvArA aMwe wirigi vaswuMxi .
Srama sAXanAlamIxa eVMwa KarcupeVdiwe vAtixvArA kUdA aMwe wirigi vaswuMxi .
SrAmikulamIxa eVMwa Karcu peVdawAdo vAri xvArA kUdA aMwe wirigi vaswuMxA , eVkkuvo wakkuvo vaswuMxA ? - ani manaM ikkada cUdAli .
100 mItarla battani wayAru ceVyyadAniki SrAmikula jIwAla mIxa .
peVttubadixArudu 20 rU. lu Karcu peVttAru .
I Karcuwo vAdu , A SrAmikula niMcI 20 kannA eVkkuva viluvani wIsukogaladani weliwe ` lABa ' rahasyaM bayatapadi poyinatte .
nijAniki iMxulo welavalasiMxemI lexu .
battani wayAru ceVyyadaMlo pAlgoVnna 3 aMSAlalonU moVxati 2 aMSAlU wama viluvakannA eVkkuva viluvani ivvalevani welipoyinappudu , A pani I 3 va aMSaM xvArAne jaruguwuMxanu kovadaMlo poVrapAtemI vuMdaxu .
A pani eVlA jaruguwuMxo mAwrame ikkada weVlusukovAli .
axi weVlusukuMte , A pani I aMSaM xvArAne jarigiMxani nirvivAxaMgA rujuvu ceVyyavaccu .
peVttubadixArudu SrAmikulaku jIwAlugA koVMwa dabbu iswAdu .
A dabbuwo SrAmikulu , AhAra paxArWAlU , battalU , axxeV illU , maMxulU vaMti vannI koVnukkuMtAru .
A vaswuvulnI SrAmikulu wama ilYlYa xaggire , wama jIvanaM kosaM vAdukuMtAru .
oVkavelYa , peVttubadixArudu , SrAmikulaku icce jIwAlu dabbu rUpaMlone gAka , vAriki kAvalasina sarukula rUpaMlone iccinA ( peVttubadixArude oVka 40 - sarukula xukANaM peVtti aMxuloMci biyyamU , battalU , maMxulU vagErAlannI SrAmikulu wIsukunelAga erpAtu ceswe ) A sarukulni kUdA SrAmikulu wama ilYlYaku wIsukupoyi ilYlYa xaggire vAdukuMtAru .
jIwAlni e rUpaMlo iccinA oVkate .
sarukule iswe A sarukule vAdukuMtAru .
dabbu iswe , xAniwo veruveru peVttubadixArula niMcI wamaku kAvalasina vaswuvulu koVnukkuni vAdukuMtAru .
eVlAgEnA jarige viRayaM oVkate .
moVxata ikkada 2 viRayAlu grahiMcAli .
( 1 ) peVttubadi xArudu SrAmikulaku ` jIwAlu ' ivvadaM aMte , vAru jIviMcadAniki kAvalasina koVnni vaswuvulu iswunnAdani arWaM .
( 2 ) jIwAlugA vuMde A vaswuvulu , peVttubadixArudi ` pani sWalAniki ' bayata SrAmikula ilYlYallo vAru jIviMcadaM kosaM KarcavuwAyi gAnI , avi SrAmikulu pani cese pani sWalaMloki vacci , akkada wayArayye saruku kosaM mudipaxArWAlU avI KarcayinattugA KarcukAvu - I 2 viRayAlU sarigA arWaM cesukuni muMxuku sAgiwe , warvAwa cUse viRayAlu cAlA weliggA vuMtAyi .
peVttubadixArudu Karcucese moVwwaM peVttubadilo oVka BAgaM ` mudipaxArWAlu ' gAnU , iMko BAgaM ` Srama sAXanAlu ' gAnU vuMtuMxi .
3va BAgaM SrAmikulaku icce ` jIwAlu ' gA vuMtuMxi .
jIwAlu aMte , SrAmikulu vAdukune vaswuvule kAbatti peVttubadilo 3va BAgaM SrAmikulu vAde vaswuvule .
I 3 BAgAle ` peVttubadi ' .
I 3 BAgAlakU saMbaMXiMcina vaswuvulu mArkeVtlo sixXaMgA wayArE lekapowe peVttubadixArudi pani sWalaMlo pane prAraMBaM kAxu .
peVttubadixArudu SrAmikulaku jIwAlu iswe ( dabbu rUpaMlo 41 - gAnI , sarukula rUpaMlo gAnI ) SrAmikulu wirigi peVttubadixArudiki emiswAru ?
biyyaM appu wIsukuni , malYlYI biyyame weVcci iccinattU , dabbu appu wIsukuni malYlYI dabbe weVcci iccinattU , peVttubadixArudi niMcI eM wIsukuMtAro wirigi ave weVcci iswArA SrAmikulu ? alA ivvadAniki vAri xaggira A vaswuvulu gAnI , A dabbugAnI eVkkada vuMtAyi ? vAtini SrAmikulu Karcu peVttesukuMtAru kAbatti peVttubadi xArudu iccina vaswuvulaku baxulugA vAru peVttubadixArudiki wama ` ' iswAru .
aMte , peVttubadixArudi pani sWalaMloki vacci vAdu ceVyyamanna ` ' ceswAru .
peVttubadixArudu , wana peVttubadilo koVMwa BAgAnni , mudi paxArWAla ' mIxa Karcu ceswe , A Karcuwo ` ' mudipaxArWAlu pani sWalaMloki vaswAyi .
peVttubadilo iMko BAgAnni ` Srama sAXanAla ' mIxa Karcu ceswe , A BAgaMwo kUdA nirjIvamEna sAXanAle pani sWalaMloki vaswAyi .

248 - vaMtacese paxXawulu sAXAraNaMgA anni AhAra paxArWAlanu viviXa rakAlEna vaMtalugA vaMdi wiMtAM .

251 - maMxa pacanaM : nItilo udaka peVttadaM valeVne I paxXawilo kUda AhArAnni nItilo vaMduwAru .

wApanAMwikalo viviXa 252 - AhAra paxArWAlu wayArayyeMxuku patte samayaM anuBavaM xvArA kUda weVluswuMxi .
nUneVlo vepadaM : AhAra paxArWAnni vaMdeMxuku udakabeVtte paxXawilo , AvirimIxa vaMdetappudu nIru e viXaMgA upayogiswAro axeviXaMgA vepadaMlo nItiki baxulu nUneVnu upayogiswAru .

10 . rAjanIwi SAswramu praBuwva pAlanA SAswramu wo eVtti saMbaMXAnni kalgivunnaxi ? lexA pAlanA , rAjakIyAla xviBAgawvaXoraNini AXunika kAlaMlo anusariMcutaku sAXyamA : rAjanIwi SAswramu . praBuwva pAlanA SAswramu : rAjyamulA XArAlanu , praBuwvanirmANa sUwrAlanu vivariMcexi rAjanIwiSAswramu .

- - 1 . ` mAtala mabbulu ' racanalo ` ' saMsWAnoxyogulanu aXikRepiMcina paxyAlunnAyi .

2 . " puRpalAvikalu " 9 paxyAlunna cinnaracana .

ivi cakkani nIwi boXakapaxyAlu .

koVMduBattIyaM : 1906 lo SrI gurajAda appArAvugAru nIlagirilo makAM cesina rojullo rAsina nAtakaM ` koVMdu BhatIyaM ' .
rElu prayANaMlo liKiwa prawi povadaM , waruvAwa 1910 lo maralA gurwuku weVccukoVni gurajAda vAru mUdu aMkAlu mAwrame wirigi rAyadaM - AMXrula xuraxqRtaM .

bilhaNIyaM : " kanyASulkaM " jAwirawnaM ayiwe ` bilhaNIyaM ' sAna pattina vajraM .
kAni AMxrajAwiki A nAtakAnni cUse axqRtaM pattalexu .

A bilhaNIyaM mareVvarU pUrwi ceyalenaMwati - kaWAkramam eVvarU gurwiMca lenaMwati - mahAkavi " - 1946 ` navoxaya lo rASAru .

meVdiltA : SrI gurajAda appArAvu gAri ` meVdiltA ' kaWa nEwikaMgA nAnAtikI pawanamOwunna oVkAnoVka xuRta vyavasWaku prawIka .

- - guwwunA muwyAlasaramulu : " guwwunA muwyAlasaramulu kUrcukoVni wetEna mAtalu koVwwa pAwala melu kalayika kroVmmeVraMgulu jimmagA " - aMtU " muwyAla sarAlu " nawnaCaMXaH sqRtiki nAMxIgIwaM pAdi rasagIwAlu vinpiMcAru mahAkavi gurajAda .

rucI , pacI leni weVlugu paxyaM geyaMgA koVwwa avawArameVwwi navanavonmeRamU , parimalYa vaMwamEnama nUwanawvAnni weVlugu kaviwvAniki saMwariMci peVttAyi muwyAla sarAlu .

" malinaxehula mAla lanucunu malinaciwwula kaXika kulamula veVlavoVsaMgina varNaXarmama Xarma XarmaMbe , maMci ceVddalu manujulaMxuna yeVMcicUdaga , reVMdeV kulamulu maMci yannaxi , mAlayEwe , mAlane , aguxun!
